# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# LLVM IR Type System to Code Generation Chain

## Your Task

Trace how LLVM IR types flow from the type creation API to code generation in llvm/llvm-project. Find C++ source files implementing: the Type class hierarchy (IntegerType, FunctionType, StructType), the type system's context ownership, and the IR type to machine type lowering in SelectionDAG.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d, sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

83-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully traced the LLVM IR type system flow from type creation to code generation and created a comprehensive answer. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Components Documented:

### 1. **Type Class Hierarchy** (IR Layer)
- **Type.h**: Base `Type` class with immutable singleton pattern
- **DerivedTypes.h**: `IntegerType`, `FunctionType`, and `StructType` implementations
- All types are created via static factory methods and uniqued per context

### 2. **Context Ownership** (Management Layer)
- **LLVMContext**: Manages type uniquing and ownership
- **LLVMContextImpl**: Contains type uniquing tables:
  - `IntegerTypes` map
  - `FunctionTypeSet` (FoldingSet)
  - `AnonStructTypes` and `NamedStructTypes`
  - `ArrayTypes`, `VectorTypes`, `PointerTypes` maps

### 3. **IR to Machine Type Conversion** (Code Generation Bridge)
- **ValueTypes.h/cpp**: `EVT` class that wraps both simple (`MVT`) and extended types
- `EVT::getEVT()`: Converts IR `Type*` to `EVT`
- `EVT::getTypeForEVT()`: Reverse conversion
- Extended types maintain pointers back to original IR types

### 4. **SelectionDAG Type Legalization** (Code Generation Layer)
- **LegalizeTypes.h**: `DAGTypeLegalizer` class managing type transformations
- Maintains transformation maps for:
  - Integer promotion/expansion
  - Float softening/promotion
  - Vector scalarization/splitting/widening
- **TargetLowering.h**: `ValueTypeActionImpl` stores target-specific type actions
- **TargetLoweringBase.cpp**: `computeRegisterProperties()` configures type actions

The complete analysis has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with files, symbols, transformation chain, and detailed narrative explanation.

Once allocated, Types are never\\n43: /// free'd.\\n44: ///\\n45: class Type {\\n46: public:\\n47:   //===--------------------------------------------------------------------===//\\n48:   /// Definitions of all of the base types for the Type system. SelectionDAG type legalization can require a\\n57:       ///< power of 2 IntegerType, so limit to the largest representable power\\n58:       ///< of 2, 8388608.\\n59:   };\\n60: \\n61:   /// This static method is the primary way of constructing an IntegerType.\\n62:   /// If an IntegerType with the same NumBits value was previously instantiated,\\n63:   /// that instance will be returned. This is 0xFF for i8, 0xFFFF for i16, etc.\\n78:   uint64_t getBitMask() const {\\n79:     return ~uint64_t(0UL) >> (64-getBitWidth());\\n80:   }\\n81: \\n82:   /// Return a uint64_t with just the most /// For example, this is 0xFF for an 8 bit integer, 0xFFFF for i16, etc.\\n89:   /// @returns a bit mask with ones set for all the bits of this type.\\n90:   /// Get a bit mask for this type.\\n91:   LLVM_ABI APInt getMask() const;\\n92: \\n93:   /// Methods for support type inquiry through isa, cast, and dyn_cast.\\n94:   static bool classof(const Type *T) {\\n95:     return T->getTypeID() ==
